***korst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:korst.html>korst</a> (18593)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">corste</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crusta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A crust, a scab <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hard, often flaky outer layer</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>

***kost.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kost.html>kost</a> (945)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cost</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">cost</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kost.html>kost</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kosten.html>kosten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kostje.html>kostje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>cost, price</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> expenses</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">used absolutely, with definite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> board, livelihood, meals and lodgings</li>
<li>food, nourishment</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kostelijk.html>kostelijk</a> (22807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kost.html>kost</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kostelijk.html>kostelijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kostelijk.html>kostelijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">kostelijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fantastic, enjoyable

***koster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>koster</a> (28671)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coster</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">costre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">custor</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">custos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>koster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>kosters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>kostertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a churchwarden, a caretaker at a church.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>Koster</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">kosterswoning</span></li></ul>

***kot.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kot</a> (38109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cote</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:cota.html>cota</a></i> (in place names), <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kota</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">little house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kutą</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kutan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably of Non-Indo-European origin, but possibly borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi">kota</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>, house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hungarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hungarian language">Hungarian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hu">ház</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finno-Ugric_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Finno-Ugric languages">Proto-Finno-Ugric</a></span>/<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="urj-pro">*kota</i>.  However, compare Dutch and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cot</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cote</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kate.html>Kate</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kot</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kotten</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koten.html>koten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kotje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">kotteke</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bad, ramshackle housing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kot.html>kot</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:woont.html>woont</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a shack she <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> in!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>rudimentary building to store (garden) material</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> student room
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Leuvense <b><a href = vnd.unilang:koten.html>koten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:brandden.html>brandden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaren.html>jaren</a> 90.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Student <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a> in Louvain burned down often in the nineties.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkamer</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">studentenkot</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>kou</a> (3336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>koude</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coude</i>, alteration (based on the adjective) of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">kelde</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*keldi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaldį̄</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kälte</i>.

***koud.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> (818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cout</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kalt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kaldaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gel-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***koudwatervrees.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koudwatervrees.html>koudwatervrees</a> (54074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> water</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrees.html>vrees</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koudwatervrees.html>koudwatervrees</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>excessive fear or trepidation about beginning something, fear of getting one's <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cousenbant</i>. The sense “yardlong bean” originated in Surinamese Dutch.

***kozak.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kozak.html>kozak</a> (29845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">cosaque</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">каза́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">коза́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kozák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> word meaning “free <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>, wanderer”. Cognate with <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Kazakh</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraai.html>kraai</a> (12374)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crâye</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*krāia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krēǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraai.html>kraai</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraaien.html>kraaien</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraai.html>kraaitje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crow, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:corvus.html>Corvus</a> corone</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zwarte.html>zwarte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraai.html>kraai</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One of certain related <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> of the genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:corvus.html>Corvus</a></i> or of the family Corvidae.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person dressed in black.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An undertaker or undertaker's employee.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A blue <a href = vnd.unilang:pennant.html>pennant</a> indicating the presence of a navigation pilot.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraaien.html>kraaien</a> (12295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crâyen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">crāien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krēaną</i>.

<ol><li>To crow, make to sound of <a href = vnd.unilang:roosters.html>roosters</a> and certain other <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a></li>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraak.html>kraak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraak.html>kraakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<li>(<i><a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a></i>) A <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> Dutch ship type</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraak.html>kraak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraak.html>kraakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">craem</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">krām</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">krām</i>. Probably from a Slavic language. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

***kraan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraan.html>kraan</a> (6591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crāne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*crano</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kranô</i>. The senses “tap” and “crane” as a machine are both based on resemblance with the bird's neck.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraan.html>kraan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kranen.html>kranen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraantje.html>kraantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>crane <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">machine for lifting</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>tap, faucet</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">machine</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hijskraan.html>hijskraan</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tap</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fontein.html>fontein</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tap</span></li></ul>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraan.html>kraan</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kranen.html>kranen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraantje.html>kraantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crabbe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*krabba</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krab.html>krab</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krabben.html>krabben</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krab.html>krabbetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">crab</span>, crustacean of the infraorder Brachyura</li></ol>

***krabbelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krabbelen.html>krabbelen</a> (24900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A frequentative verb from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krabben.html>krabben</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>. Compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">crabble</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krabbelen.html>krabbelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to scrawl, scribble</li>
<li>to scratch continuously</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krabben.html>krabben</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***krabben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krabben.html>krabben</a> (6844)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crabben</i>, further from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krabbōną</i>, with a geminated variant of the <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krabitaz</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kreeft.html>kreeft</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lobster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to scratch.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kracht.html>kracht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">force, strength</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:proef.html>proef</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">test, trial</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***krachtterm.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krachtterm.html>krachtterm</a> (115926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kracht.html>kracht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strength, force</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">term</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">term</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in 1889.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krachtterm.html>krachtterm</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krachttermen.html>krachttermen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krachtterm.html>krachttermpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An expletive; a profane or abusive term, notably a curse, blasphemous or obscene oath. <span class="defdate">[from late 19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1889</b> December 9, S., "Letterkundige <a href = vnd.unilang:kroniek.html>kroniek</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:titel.html>titel</a>", <i>Haagsche <a href = vnd.unilang:courant.html>Courant</a></i>, No. 2069, page 2.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:professor.html>professor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> Amsterdam <a href = vnd.unilang:verklaarde.html>verklaarde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> in klassieken <a href = vnd.unilang:waanzin.html>waanzin</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:vergeef.html>vergeef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> den <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krachtterm.html>krachtterm</a></b>), <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:las.html>las</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:minstens.html>minstens</a> 10 <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oud.html>oud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <a href = vnd.unilang:professor.html>professor</a> in Amsterdam once declared in classical insanity (forgive <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> for the <b>abusive term</b>), that he never read anything that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> not at least 10 years old.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***krakeling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krakeling.html>krakeling</a> (34999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crakelinc</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krakeling.html>krakeling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krakelingen.html>krakelingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krakeling.html>krakelingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A brittle, usually sweet pretzel-shaped pastry, often a puff pastry.</li>

***kraken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a> (5518)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crāken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*krakon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krakōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crack, break open (a shell)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a creaky sound, like something being cracked</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break up into (chemical) components</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break someone mentally</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to solve a code</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive and intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to practise chiropractic (on a patient)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squat (a building)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start (<a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of the day)</li></ol>

***kraker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kraker.html>kraker</a> (37019)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraken.html>kraken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crack, break</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraker.html>kraker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krakers.html>krakers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kraker.html>krakertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who cracks or an instrument used to crack.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">chiropractor</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderzoek.html>onderzoek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kraker.html>kraker</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> to go to the <b>chiropractor</b> for an examination.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">squatter</span>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oude.html>oude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fabriek.html>fabriek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wonen.html>wonen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoned.html>stonede</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krakers.html>krakers</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:stoned.html>Stoned</a> <b>squatters</b> are now living in the old factory.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a thing of good quality, a cracker.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwachten.html>verwachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echte.html>echte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kraker.html>kraker</a></b> in Port Elizabeth.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> expect a real <b>cracker</b> (of a match) tomorrow in Port Elizabeth.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
